                 Almanach de Saxe Gotha - Online Royal Genealogical Reference Handbook

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Almanach de Saxe Gotha - The Online Royal Genealogical Reference Handbook - Der Saxe Gotha Genealogisches Handbuch des Adels - Online Genealogical Reference for Reigning and non-Reigning Royal Houses and the Princely and Ducal Families of Europe and South America, and the Diplomatic and Statistical Guide to the World. Volume - I - The Reigning - Formerly Reigning Royal Houses of Europe and South America Encompasses and Lists the Genealogy of the Imperial and Royal Sovereign Houses and Families Reigning and Formerly Reigning in Europe and South America. Volume - II - The Mediatized Sovereign Houses of the Holy Roman Empire of the German Nation Encompasses and lists the genealogy of the Mediatised Sovereign Houses of the Holy Roman Empire of the German Nation. Volume - III - The Non-Sovereign Princely and Ducal Houses of Europe Encompasses and lists the Genealogy of The Non-Sovereign Princely and Ducal Houses and Families of Europe. Volume - IV - The Nobility of the Holy Roman Empire Encompasses and Lists the Imperial Nobility of Holy Roman Empire of the German Nation to the present day in Parts: I - II - III- IV - V Volume - V - The British Peerage System Gotha Index to the British Peerage System, the formal listing of the Titles, Ranks, Styles, Title Holders and their Heirs, the Date of Creation and the Present Status of the Peerage listed (I): Dukes - Marquesses - Earls (II): Viscounts (III - A-B): Barons and Lords (IV): Baronets. Volume - VI - The Royal Families of the World Encompasses the History and lists the Genealogy of the Royal Houses and Families of the World - 2019. Volume - VII - The Higher European Nobility Encompasses and lists the Genealogy of The Gotha Higher Nobility of Europe to the present day - I-XVI Volume - VIII - The Nobility of the World Index of the Nobility of the World, the History and Register of Nobility and the formal listing of the Titles and Ranks of Nobility in the World.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Taken Community
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome TAKEN Family.... After over 20 years of being happily #Taken, my wife and I have decided to make it our mission to empower couples to master marriage. Even though we’ve been very blessed by God, we’ve also faced some big challenges in our marriage — like financial struggles, family drama, and even life threatening illness. Because of that, we know how hard it is to go through tough times – especially when you feel alone. That’s why we created The Taken Community – to help couples through their struggles so they can come out stronger on the other side. By joining The Taken Community, not only do you receive inspirational content and advice, but you become a part of a family here to support you and celebrate with you in the good times and the bad. If you’re someone who wants to bring their best self to their relationship, or is looking for help, we invite you to join us.

                 WELCOME NEW MEMBERS! PLEASE READ BEFORE POSTING: (1)👉If you disagree with someone, please do so respectfully. There's enough rudeness and profanity elsewhere on Facebook. (2)👉Your post will be approved only when it is your original meme/content.(priority for OC) (3)👉Spammers will be autoclaved. (4)👉Absolutely no advertising or commercial posts. (5)👉We reserve the right to occasionally post links to products that we believe may be of interest to group members. (6)👉Shared posts from other pages/groups will be deleted. (7)👉DO NOT ask questions that are easily answered by a Google search. (8)👉NO political or religious-themed posts will be approved, However, you may express your opinions in comments so long as they are respectful. In short you cannot defame or promote any party agenda or face here . (9)👉No nudity/porn related post/links will be approved. (10)👉We will remove any posts or comments that are hateful or Offensive (i.e., sexist, racist, homophobic, etc.). (11)👉If a post evokes controversy, we will remove it if is reported more than twice and if more than half the comments are negative. ******************************************** *Please do report any users that are posting hateful comments. You can DM us by sending a FB message. We will ban users who consistently post comments that have profanity and that are obviously offensive or abusive in any way. ******************************************* IF YOUR POST IS NOT APPROVED: Bear in mind the following. •The most important thing is "your post should be original". • Images in memes need to be good quality. • Post/meme should be in English. •We prefer original content and not shared from other pages. If you think your post is/are deleting by mods and it's appropriate do mention the Admin. We'll take Action on concern Mods. Thanks for your attention &lt;3

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Scottish/British Names &amp; Family group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for those wanting to share information about Scottish or British names and connections to family history. Help is available from group members and genealogists, Douglas Moncrieff and Valerie Prince. Our sister groups are Scottish history and Culture, found here: http://facebook.com/groups/scothistory/ And for everything else, Clan Scotland: https://www.facebook.com/groups/clanscotland/ * We regret that due to privacy laws, we are unable to assist in finding living persons. Please do not post personal data for any living person in our group. * Posts or comments not pertaining to family name history, genealogy, and name research may be deleted at admin's sole discretion. * Advertising products/services and spamming are not permitted; such posts/comments will result in immediate expulsion from the group. * Uncivil discourse may be warned, deleted, and group members may be deleted, at admin's sole discretion. * If a friend or family member is interested in joining our group, please have him or her make the request from their own account. We will not accept requests submitted by third parties. This ensures that only interested people are members of our group. * Questions about group rules should only be directed to an admin's private messages, not posted in the group. Thank you!
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 GAY FOR GOOD - L.A. MEMBERS
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 “GAY FOR GOOD – Los Angeles” (the first chapter of "GAY FOR GOOD" was founded in the Fall of 2008) - "Gay For Good aims to energize and mobilize the LGBT community to interact with the greater Los Angeles community by volunteering our time to various social welfare and environmental service projects. TO RECEIVE ALL MEMBERSHIP INFO SIGN UP AT WWW.GAYFORGOOD.ORG Each month, we select a different non-profit to donate our time for a community service project. No money involved - just donate your time - do something valuable for the city while meeting other great members of the LGBT community and the community at large! PROJECTS Gay For Good: LA – provides over 250 hours of service each month to local service projects in LA. Below are a examples of some of our past events in 2009. ---------- Interested in expansion, please contact: tony.biel@gayforgood.org ---------- EXAMPLES OF PAST PROJECTS: JANUARY - "Tree People" http://www.treepeople.com FEBRUARY - "LA FOODBANK" http://www.lafoodbank.org MARCH - Tree People http://www.treepeople.com APRIL - Friends of Ballona Wetlands http://www.ballonafriends.org/ MAY - LA RIVER CLEAN-UP http://folar.org/ JUNE - "Friends of Lockwood" JULY - West Hollywood Community Housing Corp. http://www.whchc.org AUGUST – HEAL THE BAY http://www.healthebay.org SEPTEMBER – ANIMAL ADVOCATES http://www.animaladvocatesalliance.org OCTOBER - RUNYON CANYON RESTORATION http://laparks.org 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ancestry website users
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 For users of the Ancestry website (All regions are welcome) and the Ancestry mobile app, to share questions and find answers in the mechanics of using the website and the mobile app. The group concentrates on the genealogy aspect of using the Ancestry Website, finding the documents to support your tree. For how to really delve deep into the DNA, you will find multitudes of other groups geared towards DNA. Admin and moderator folks have no connection to Ancestry at all, other than being a user of the website, strictly volunteers. Ancestry .com is not associated with this facebook page. With that in mind, please understand it is not a group to bash Ancestry or the companies that have working platforms with Ancestry (IE, rootsMagic and Family Tree Maker, for starters). You have an issue you need help working through, sure, that is absolutely what we are here for. Just to go an a rampage about how much you don't like Ancestry and don't like the changes, no, this is not the group for that. In other words, No Venting. There is a group facebook post to make suggestions for changes and please bring this back requests. Again, please keep it civil when making the suggestions and requests. Please keep questions related to things about using Ancestry and the software that links to the site. This is not a search group for finding living family members. If you need help on how to search for your long passed family, then this is your group. There are two sets of Units required before you first post. You will have to agree to those in the questions asked you request to join this group. there are short tutorials on the workings of this group and and even quicker set on ways to better navigate facebook. There are, also, several other non-mandatory units on ways to use ancestry. Ancestry corp folks may join, but *please* identify yourself to the group.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Medieval Genealogy Society
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Medieval Genealogy Society is here to share and have fun! Many of us have been able to trace our ancestors into the Medieval era, and thus, been able to discover amazing stories about our past and about history! This is the place to share those stories, but also to share any tips about the process of genealogy. So join us and have a bit of fun! You don't have to have links to Medieval ancestors--just an interest in the era and in family history is all you need! Share with your friends so we can build a community! (YOU MUST ANSWER THE QUESTIONS TO BE ADMITTED)

                 CHEROKEE INDIANS - RESEARCH/GENEALOGY
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  A. It is YOUR responsibility to provide the basic info required, as provided in EVERYONE'S post. B. DO NOT CONTACT the admins or researchers. . We do not do research through private messages C-If anyone wants to invite friends to the page please send them the link to the page and they can request to join. Invites will not be accepted . Also check out the other announcements here . *********Postings of DNA results will not be allowed . DNA tests have no relevancy to finding Cherokee ancestry or for enrollment purposes. DNA can be used to find paternal lines************* &lt;&lt;&lt;-=-&gt;&gt;&gt; DO NOT INTERRUPT SOMEONE'S THREAD FOR A RESEARCH REQUEST OR UNRELATED ITEM&lt;&lt;&lt;-=-&gt;&gt;&gt; 1-Cherokee Indians - research + a genealogy research IS A FREE CHEROKEE RESEARCH SITE. NO FEE IS CHARGED FOR THE RESEARCH FOR AND ABOUT CHEROKEE . 2-A thread will be started for your individual research WHEN YOU MAKE A REQUEST FOR RESEARCH WITH THE BASIC INFORMATION REQUESTED FOR EVERYONE. Documents will be posted for you and others who may be following. If there is no response to a thread (24 hour window) that was started that thread may be deleted and UNRESPONSIVE will be added to the original request. The person may also be removed from the group. Communication is important. This will also be added to the announcement section. 3-ANYONE CLAIMING TO BE CHEROKEE MAY BE ASKED WHO THAT PERSONS FAMILY IS 4-ANYONE WITHOUT A PROFILE PICTURE WILL NOT BE ACCEPTED 5-We DO NOT endorse NOR do we promote groups of people in fake or Cherokee State "tribes". We DO NOT permit "truck-stop" Indian-styled "art" with fake "Native American" sayings or other unrelated posts from other pages that may contain a virus or click bait . All such posts will be deleted as well as the person who posted it. 6-DO NOT INTERRUPT ANOTHER PERSONS THREAD.......THAT COMMENT CAN GET DELETED**. 7- IF ANYONE BLOCKS AN ADMIN OR MODERATOR THEY WILL BE REMOVED/BANNED FROM THE GROUP 8- PLEASE BE SPECIFIC ABOUT THE DOCUMENTS THAT ARE MENTIONED. IF THE PERSON IS ON A ROLL NAME THE ROLL ALONG WITH THE NUMBER/LINK. 9-POSTS/PEOPLE WILL BE DELETED FOR THOSE WHO CONTINUE TO IGNORE THESE DIRECTIONS. 10- USE OF PROFANITY IS NOT ALLOWED ESPECIALLY THE "F" BOMB. THAT WILL GET YOU BANNED.

Rules For The Group: • Be kind. No profanity or personal attacks. • No promotional posting of any kind. • No posting articles, videos, music, or links. • No 'venting' comments that are negative. • Posts must be short (250 words or less).               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 FREE OBITUARY LOOK UPS
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WELCOME, Obituaries can be extremely helpful in genealogy and we look forward to helping you locate your requests :) (THIS GROUP SERVES TWO PURPOSES) 1) IT IS FOR PERSONAL OBITUARY REQUESTS TO ASSIST YOU IN FURTHERING YOUR GENEALOGY RESEARCH 2) IT IS ALSO FOR GROUP MEMBERS TO HELP OTHERS WITH HIS/HER REQUESTS IF AND WHEN POSSIBLE) What makes this group unique???? 1) There is not another one like it. :) 2) Each request is viewed by admin and all volunteers within the state requested. If a request can be located through online resources, it is usually posted within a couple days. :) 3) Each state has it's own volunteers and people that are willing to assist. (including accessing papers not available to the public online, going to the local library in the area the death took place, and using other resources in the state the death took place which are not accessible online) 4) There are times an Admin will place a library request for a member if all information is provided and an online library form is available. However, it is best if you are given a library referral to follow the link and make the request as Admins can often get extremely busy. 5) There are several helpful links provided to assist everyone in every state with research. 6) Obituaries are saved so the search is not duplicated and to assist others researching the same family/person. These can be found on the following Facebook page. https://www.facebook.com/ObituaryandDeathNotices/ 7) This group is very structured and monitored daily and we respond to every request. Once you become a member, please read The top "pinned" post in this group. It will provide a full explanation of the group, rules, etc. We ONLY cover the United States. We no longer cover Canada as there is a group dedicated for that. Always remember to be patient and be kind as it takes time to locate obituaries. Enjoy!!! Thank you :) If you want to join/share the group use hashtag #FreeObituaryLookups Please consider a donation for site services which includes unlimited obituary requests and access to all group information/etc. You can do this by following the link below and hit the "Shop Now" button to donate) Every donation helps :) Thank you https://www.facebook.com/ObituaryandDeathNotices/ Thank you in advance :)

NO PROFESSIONAL ADVICE MAY BE GIVEN TO ANY MEMBER, if you are a lawyer, doctor, therapist, etc, we appreciate your contributions, but it is against most state laws, and Facebook policy to provide this type of information. 10. Roll call posts will be posted by the admin team on a weekly basis. Please do not post your own. No mentions of locations allowed. 12. We take suicide very seriously. Threats may be reported to facebook here. https://www.facebook.com/help/contact/305410456169423 If you are struggling please reach out to one of the hotlines below. National Suicide Prevention Hotline 1-800-273-8255 Call 911 or 1-800-SUICIDE 1-800-273-TALK TTY 1-800-799-4TTY Military Veterans Suicide Hotline: 1-800-273-TALK LGBT Youth Suicide Hotline: 1-866-4-U-TREVOR In the UK or Republic of Ireland: Call Samaritans 116123
                </div>

We do not allow pornography, No solicitation of any kind are permitted !,Ready to say "I Do" do not attain any personal meeting outside the group or Do not obtain any legal obligations of any kind.The usage of FOUL language will not be Tolerated.We are all mature adults any disrespect of any kind will not be tolerated. Some of the views that are posted are not necessarily the views of the group of Ready to say "I Do" in its entirety. Remember this is a Christian Based Group, teaching Christian Marriage fundamentals to become and prepare each and everyone for Marriage. To all members of Ready to say " I DO " Please do not post any business ads, personal ads, or opportunity ads in the group. ALL POSTINGS of this kind will be deleted.

                 Heirloom's Lost, Found &amp; Returned
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Facebook Group TERMS OF SERVICE: (as of August 01, 2019) By using our Facebook Groups, you agree to the following: The purpose of the group is to reunite lost family heirlooms, memorabilia and the like with current living family members, as well as share genealogical and historical information and to help others in researching family history. This is not an adoption group. We strictly adhere to the group guidelines so please read them after you are added, if you do not agree do not stay as a member. The group is continually monitored, violations will result in removed posts without a courtesy message. All members are screened to eliminate fake profiles and spammers. If you have concerns please send a message to an admin, do not post to the group wall. This page is moderated. Posts judged by the administrators of this forum to be inappropriate, adversely negative or that do not otherwise serve the purpose of this page’s creation will be removed without notice. Members who post inappropriate material may also be removed and / or banned from the group without notice. While Heirloom Archaeology finds, researches and returns lost family heirlooms at no cost, this does not prevent its members from requesting compensation when preforming the same services. However, any other solicitation of money in Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned Group is strictly prohibited. Any member post that incites “trolling” on any and all Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned related groups will be deleted without warning. Trolling includes any and all posts that include a form of harassment or destructive language with the intent to provoke another member into destructive or negative comments. This includes all politically biased posts, blatant advertisements, embedded links, financial call to action posts as well as posts with sexual content. If you have a gripe or complaint with a member of this page, please discuss with that person on another site or via private means. No one enjoys the negativity. As part of our effort to keep the page positive, we’ve decided Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned should remain a politically-neutral place. Therefore, we ask members not utilize the site to instigate political debate among members. Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned does not allow MLM (Multi Level Marketing) advertisements on our Facebook Group and are at the discretion of the moderators, but include calls to action soliciting sales representatives. Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned does not allow contests, including calls to action to do a particular task, in order to get something in return. Cursing on Heirloom’s Lost, Found &amp; Returned in any form, is cause for the user to immediately be banned. This Group cannot be all things to all people. This page was created to foster a positive environment; it does not mean there is not a place to voice a complaint … it’s just not here. If you see a post that should not be here, simply send a message to an administrator.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Divorce &amp; Separation Support Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Relationship break down is high up on the list of life's most stressful events. It's an isolating period meandering your way through this minefield, emotionally, financially and legally. The aim of this group is to share and support so that those effected can ask for advice on any aspect of relationship break down and better still for people to offer advice and tips on getting through it.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 True Love💙
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Love. It makes the world go 'round, right? Well, at least that's the how the saying goes. But is it true? It should be, but so many people confuse love with things like jealousy or possessiveness. True love isn't either of those things. But these 16 things are. So here are the characteristics of REAL love: 1. Love means saying goodbye to expectations. Sure, we all want people to behave the way we want them to. We want them to be more affectionate. Or more outgoing. Or smarter. Or more ambitious. All of these things are expectations. Expectations are just your requirements for "acceptability" of loving someone. But true love has no expectations. It simply loves "as is." 2. Love doesn't play the victim role or blame others. Love doesn't think others are "out to get them." Love doesn't think their loved ones are wrong. Love works together. It takes responsibility. It forgives and allows other people's actions to be their journey. Love doesn't take things personally. includes letting go. Love doesn't equal possession. Just as the saying goes, "If you love something, set it free. If it comes back, it's yours. If it doesn't, then it never was." There is truth to that. Love allows people their freedom. It doesn't hold tightly and crush their wings in attempt to keep them. True love doesn't want to possess. It is willing to set you free if you want to be. 4. Love doesn't require you to continue a relationship. You may love someone very much, but you may not be compatible with them. Or they may drive you crazy with their continued disregard for your feelings. You can still love them, but that doesn't mean you have to be with them. Love doesn't mean that you have to stay, and stay and stay. You can leave the relationship and love them anyway. 5. Love has no room for jealousy. Like possession, jealousy doesn't equal love. We think that if we're not jealous of our loved ones that it means that we don't love them. True love has confidence in the quality of the relationship. It knows that the other person is happy and content coming back to you and only you. 6. Love is the absence of fear. You can put all emotions on a continuum. On one end, you have love. Then appreciation. After that, it's joy, happiness, contentment and satisfaction. On the opposite end of the continuum of love is fear. Other fear-based emotions include, hatred, insecurity, jealousy or greed. 
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">29&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">0 篇新帖</span></span>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Lithuanian Global Genealogical Society
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 LGGS is a non-profit society that provides a website and several Internet groups for the use of LGGS members, fellow genealogists, and those just starting their research on Lithuania, and family genealogy. Our mission is to collect, preserve, and disseminate knowledge and information about Lithuanian genealogical and related historical, biographical, and heraldic data; to inculcate and promote interest in accurate research in these fields; to issue publications in various forms of media; and to encourage, promote, and provide genealogical education and scholarly training for all interested in these endeavors.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 LGBTQ Heritage/Memorial Project
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 If you've ever looked at your family tree, you've undoubtedly noticed inexplicable "dead-ends." Some are easily explained as people who passed away at a young age, before they had a chance to grow new "branches." A few are probably just people who, for one reason or another, never married or had offspring... a personal choice. But I believe that many of these were our LGBTQ Aunts, Uncles, and cousins, for whom there was never a classification, nor historic record (marriage certificate, birth of offspring, public record, etc.). It is my intention to change that. While we can't force these "dead ends" to sprout new branches, we can fill them in with "leaves." I want us to name them, share family portraits, memories, any details we can find, so that their lives no longer lack meaning. "We live as long as we are remembered." ~ Russian proverb
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Croatian Heritage and Genealogy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The group is meant for a place to learn and share information and, perhaps most importantly were families and friends may connect. 1) Recipes and other useful information can be found in the FILES section - please feel free to add a recipe. 2) When posting a query about a SURNAME or individual please let us know what info you have found so far. 3) You may post anything to do with Croatian Heritage or Genealogy. 4) To begin new topic go to the very top of the page where it says "Write something.." 5) we reserve the right remove any post we deem offensive or off topic. And for those who need help I can offer genealogy services as well we have 2 Croatia based genealogists: Sanja Frigan Ciuha http://www.croatianroots.com/ Lidija Sambunjak http://www.croatian-genealogy.com/ And if you have never been to Croatia, Sue and I take small groups on Heritage Tours of Croatia. Our next Heritage Tours to Croatia will be Sept 2018, May 2019 and Advent Season/Christmas Market 2019. Click on this link for more details including dates and pricing. http://www.protrav.com/leisure-vacation-travel/professional-travel-vacations/heritage-tour-of-croatia/ Please be courteous – and please follow these simple rules of this group While most of us have opinions on politics... This is NOT the group for politics. Any political posts will be deleted. We do NOt allow the following: 1) NO political posts nor political discussions 2) NO commercial postings 3) NO swearing nor foul language 4) NO derogatory comments about any ethnic group nor religious group If you choose to ignore the above rules, you will be removed from the group, immediately, no questions asked. If you disagree then this is NOT the group for you. Thank you for joining us and Please enjoy! Croatian Heritage and Genealogy Facebook Group Founded January 28, 2014 by Robert and Suzanne Jerin

                 Help with relationships, marriage and dating
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for help with relationships, dating, and marriage. We are here to help, give advice and support, just post it in the group and we will try our best to help you. This group is NOT an advertising group! NO SPAMMING! If you are looking for someone to date, this is not the right group for you. Not a go fund me site or group. RULES: 1. Be Kind and Courteous We're all in this together to create a welcoming environment. Let's treat everyone with respect. Healthy debates are natural, but kindness is required. 2. No Hate Speech or Bullying Make sure everyone feels safe. Bullying of any kind isn't allowed, and degrading comments about things like race, religion, culture, sexual orientation, gender or identity will not be tolerated. 3. No Promotions or Spam Give more than you take to this group. Self-promotion, spam and irrelevant links aren't allowed. 4. Respect Everyone's Privacy Being part of this group requires mutual trust. Authentic, expressive discussions make groups great, but may also be sensitive and private. What's shared in the group should stay in the group.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello and Welcome! PLEASE NOTE: WE ARE A STRICT GENEALOGY GROUP! This group is all about Discovering Your Family History! Would you like to ask questions, or share what you have found? When helping, please be courteous. A lot of our members are just beginning. This is one of the fastest growing genealogy groups. Each day you can find assistance with your research problems, or offer your expertise to someone who is stuck. Join hundreds of women and men just like you who are finding their ancestors. The purpose of this group is to assist members in research ancestors - to learn about resources and techniques that will enhance that research. Basic Rules (Please read the full rules when joining): 1. No searching for or discussing living people 2. No selling goods or services (even if genealogy related) 3. Venting is discouraged. 4. Do not post you photos in this group. 5. Do not post downloaded newpaper images from subscription sites. Post the link instead. Please read the remainder of the rules: https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=1878627885514670&amp;set=gm.1844421528941857&amp;type=3&amp;theater Looking for a specific State, Country or Topic? Other Genealogy! Just Ask! Groups: http://www.genealogyjustask.com/ 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Wife Diaries
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Wife Diaries™ was founded by Shanae M. Johnson in July 2011, to provide a positive platform exclusively for wives to feel comfortable discussing the trials and triumphs of marriage while lending and receiving advice on all related topics. With over 13,500 wives world-wide, and over 100 diary entries per day, Wife Diaries has ballooned into a movement where wives are interacting with one another on this private Facebook group page and sharing entries on everything from recipes, pregnancy and infidelity to beauty trends, fitness, children and more. Friendships have since exceeded the virtual realm through “Wives’ Night Out” events hosted by regional Wife Diaries representatives. The only requirement to join Wife Diaries is that you are a women who is currently legally married and are seeking to establish stronger bonds with other women who face similar highs and lows with their spouse. This is a closed group, therefore only the wives (group members) see the posts. If you would like to post anonymously, we offer that as well. Please feel free to request to join the group. Once you are in, spread the word to other wives so that they can join the conversation as well. If you have any questions, comments, or concerns please direct them to admin@wifediaries.com ***PLEASE READ RULES*** 1. NO SCREENSHOTTING: Do not capture members posts and share them. This is our diary and safe place. 2. NO NAME CALLING: Do not call any members out of their name. 3. NO FLOODING THE PAGE WITH SHARES FROM OTHER PAGES THAT AREN’T MARRIAGE RELATED 4. NO FOLLOWUP POSTS: If your post was deleted, it was done for a reason. Please message an admin if you have any concerns. 5. NO RUDE RESPONSES: There is a difference between offering genuine advice and being nasty. Think before you speak. 6. NO NUDE OR SEXUALLY EXPLICIT PHOTOS OR VIDEOS 7. NO GO FUND ME REQUESTS unless approved by shanae@wifediaries.com 8. NO PROMOTING OF GROUPS RELATED TO WD: it’s a conflict of interest. Also, do not add WD members to other marriage groups without their knowledge. 9. Personal business ads are prohibited in the main forum. All ads may be placed in the in the WD Business Pages. 10. DO NOT share personal member stories outside of the group with non-WD members. This is our safe place. If this occurs, you will be removed immediately. ***You will get 3 chances. If you violate the rules, you will be banned from the group*** Wife Diaries purpose is to encourage, not discourage. We encourage you to "Like" our public page www.facebook.com/pages/Wife-Diaries and visit our website www.wifediaries.com

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Our Sephardic Family
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Background Our Sephardic Family is a Facebook group created in 2011 by Mark Angel. It has grown to 4000+ members on 6 continents. This group is comprised mainly of Sephardic members, but others have joined because of their interest Sephardiem are descendants of Jews fled from the Iberian Peninsula (what is now Spain and Portugal). Vision The vision of this group is to share our heritage and to better understand our mutual Sephardic history. Our goal is to connect Sephardics, and strengthen the concept of family and common cultural bonds. We hope to share knowledge of our precious customs, foods, dress, language and rituals so we leave empowered and inspired through our culture. This will contribute toward our future legacy and help preserve precious Sephardic heritage. Interesting demographics about Our Sephardic Family: Total number of countries: 67 ---- Top 10 countries represented: United States,Israel,Turkey,South Africa,Mexico,United Kingdom,Canada,Brazil,Belgium,France ---- Gender: Male~40% ; Female~60%
                </div>

                 Poly + Mono Relationships
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Poly + Mono Relationships is a support group for polyamorous and monogamous partners to discuss issues relating to poly/mono mixed relationships. General discussion is encouraged as a way to share with others in the community, but please adhere to Group Rules in the About section. As discussions of relationships can sometimes be of a frank and explicit nature, membership is restricted to people of age 18 and above. P+M is a "closed" group and only other group members can see that you are in this group and any posts and comments you make. If you have any questions or concerns, please message an admin. If you receive no reply within a couple of hours, create a post here stating that you've sent a message. Blocking any of the admins interferes with official communications and doing so will lead to being removed from the group.                  MEMBER GUIDELINES: (1) The mission of this group is to encourage genealogical discovery, to share genealogy related information, and to help one another in our genealogical research. (5) Do not post product promotions -- with the exception of notices about books, films, and events that are genealogy related. (6) We urge you to visit and join the OBA website: www.ourblackancestry.com If you violate the guidelines, you will be deleted from membership without notice.

No promotional posting whatsoever. 2. No bashing, judgment or putting others down- this is a safe place to open up. Judgment goes counter to that principle. 3.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Gay Fathers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 All dads and hopeful dads are welcome. Please refrain from the following: (1) any post asking for money/fundraising; (2) any post requesting help in with facebook likes to your page or a contest/promotion (promotions may be posted with admin prior approval); (3) negativity or criticism of others' opinions or parenting style that are unsolicited; (4) posting of surveys for data without permission (note surveys about parenting and family issues are welcome, but please send a copy via messaging to an admin); (5) trolling or negative statements; (6) oversharing of curated content from other FB pages and websites (memes, quotes, etc.); (7) criticism of parenthood path (adoption, surrogacy, marriage, etc.), faith or geographic region; (8) posts that have no relation to gay fatherhood or links to stories that are best shared on your personal page; (9) posts to cause conflict, dissonance or separation among group members; (10) personal vents, requesting support is fine, however using the page as your personal counselor is not a best practice; (11) remember this is a closed group and if you wish to share something from this group outside of this group, please get the permission of the original poster. (12) Commenting on the appearance of any father's child or any minor in a sexualized way will not be tolerated and will result in removal from group with no warning. (13) Posting photos of yourself without kids is often viewed in the group as self-serving and desiring comments on your appearance. Keep your selfies and personal pics for your personal page. (14) While we encourage friendships among our members, bear in mind that many members prefer to keep closer boundaries. If you PM a member and are asked to stop, continuing to send messages will invalidate your group membership. Due to the volunteer nature of this board, private notification of removal will not be provided. If you ever have a question as to why something was removed, please privately message an admin with the general content or attachment. Public admonishment of the volunteer team isn't a best practice. Any person bringing more negativity than good to the overall group experience will be removed without warning. Use wisdom when connecting within and outside the community. Our community management team values your family's safety, mental health, and financial wellness. As you connect with others in the community (publicly in the group, in real life, in private messages, mentorship program, etc.) please use caution. With the rise of fake profiles, predators, and "cons," please approach every interaction with good judgment. The admins of Gay Fathers are not responsible for any loss or damage resulting from connections created here, directly or indirectly. We have the highest level of member screening and approval available on facebook, however, some slip through the process due to the nature of what they do and their motives for joining.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Genealogy and DNA for Beginners
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Genealogy and DNA for Beginners is a fun group for those starting or relatively new to genealogical research. We even give away free gifts! :) Feel free to ask any questions but please always use the Group search function before asking a question. Please read the pinned post at the top of the group before your first post. On mobile devices click "show pinned post". This is a zero-spam zone. Please do not try to sell anything here. Do not post promotional links to your own blogs or other Facebook groups or sites such as Amazon. 1. Ask lots of questions. Everyone wants to help you grow. 2. Please do not post ANY non-relevant links. 3. Please do not try to sell anything in the group. This means your own products/services or those of others. 4. Please be kind and respectful toward your fellow members. This includes staying on topic and avoiding politics. 5. If we no longer serve your purposes and you choose to leave, we wish you well. 6. If you are stuck or have a problem, please ask. 7. If anyone private messages you offering to sell you something, block them and let us know. 8. If we post an item we recommend, please do not tell everyone it's expensive. If it's not for you then don't say anything. 9. If you want to follow a post, come into the group and go to the upper right hand corner of the post and click Turn on Notifications. Please do not type F, . , or following. 10. From time to time we may post links to products/services we think of value. You may assume that some of these links are affiliate links. We only recommend products we believe in and/or have personally used ourselves. 11. We are a participant in the Amazon Services LLC Associates Program, an affiliate advertising program designed to provide a means for us to earn fees by linking to Amazon.com and affiliated sites. 12. Do not post copyrighted or confidential documents. If you do need to ask for help deciphering handwriting then please crop the image down to the specific words. 13. Do not add people to the group. They will not be processed. 14. We understand that sometimes you may want to tell the group about a good deal, service or product you've seen. If this is the case then create a post and start it with "ADMIN". We will review the link in your post and, if approved, re-post it as an admin post. We're often asked about a good book regarding DNA and genetic research. We heartily recommend you get a copy of Blaine T. Bettinger's best-seller on this topic, available on Amazon at this link: https://amzn.to/2EMIAiY Love, Darren, Julie.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is dedicated to those doing genealogical research of their Sicilian ancestors. RULES: *Keep posts related to Sicilian genealogy(see note*). *Family photos and their stories are encouraged ! (see note*) *Do not add a color background to your post, or memes or GIFs in your comments. *If you ask for a recommendation, please remove the 'map' that FB automatically adds and the recommendation links, and the preview for Ancestry(dot)com.* These take up too much room and interfere with searches. *Please post the URL/link to an image when asking for a translation.* *No advertising, direct or indirect, or blocking an admin or moderator. *No promoting your blog, books, videos, etc. * If you add/invite your friends, then tell them, and to click the join button and answer the questions, otherwise, the invite will be deleted. *Professionals may NOT post with ANY link to/from their business/business page, etc. or solicit in any way = removal. *No promoting of other groups, politics, blogs, *culture posts, etc. *Any file you create will be deleted over time. * NOTE: We love to hear about your trips, your traditions, your family and photos, recipes, and your genealogical successes!* It's about FAMILY here. *PHOTOS: when posting several photos, please do it in ONE post, or add them as comments under your original post. Posting them individually takes up too much room and interferes with searches. *Add a note to not share your photo without permission, if that is a concern for you*. NOTE: We are an open group, in which persons deceased 70+ years are discussed. This is, by law, public info. If you have problems not wanting info seen, I can help you privately, or post anonymously for you. The administrators reserve the prerogative to remove/delete any and all posts and comments that are not in keeping with the objective of this group. This is not open to discussion. *IMPORTANT: Click the words "3 comments" under the pinned post' ( the red/yellow box) to access the surname and comune spreadsheet.* The first comment by Alex, is the one with the spreadsheet - read the instructions. You can tag him in a post if you have any questions. *If someone donates their time to help you find information, make a translation or whatever - PLEASE take the time to personally and graciously THANK that person and NOT with the abbreviation "TY" or a thumbs up. Members in ANY group work for gratitude, and it is needed for them to continue to be helpful! *Notifications from the group can be controlled from the notification tab under our group's photo, or from one of the posts in your news feed (if you want to unfollow, but still remain in the group). Check the files tab, and the photo albums tab for helpful resources! DO NOT share files that I have given my time to create for use in this group ! Good luck with your research and have fun exploring the group, files and photo albums!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 :ايها الأعضاء الجدد ‎السلام عليكم واهلا بكم في الجروب. ‎ الاعترافات الشخصية و الأسئلة لغرض واحد فقط هو مساعدة بعضنا البعض في الإشياء التي يصعب البوح عنها . الكل هنا لاخذ الاّراء فى مساعدة غيرهم علي طريقة ايجابية تحترم او الرد باحترام. وسوف يتم إنزال عدد محدود من ال posts يوميا سيعطى الجميع فرصة لتلقى الردود عليها وقضايا اخرى للتفاعل. اذا كان لديك اية اقتراحات او افكار او شكاوى او المسائل المتصلة بالجروب فا رجاء لا تتردد فى الاتصال بالمسؤولين. ‎1. محتويات الجروب 21+ خاصة ولا يمكن مشاركتها مع اى شخص خارج الجروب لضمان الخصوصية والامان. ‎2. فقط الاعترافات و المناقشات الجادة التي تتعلق بالفكر العام للجروب سيتم نشرها. ‎3. الوظائف الجنسية تشكل نسبة كبيرة من المحتوى و نشرها لغرض طلب المساعدة. لا تعكس شخصية المسؤولين او معتقداتهم او أيديولوجيتهم ولكنها تشترك فى الحالة الوحيدة للمساعدة وليس تشجيع ‎4. المناقشات على اساس الاراء السياسية او الدينية غير مرغوبة. ‎5. لا يسمح للاعلانات الشخصية ‎6. بالنسبة للمواقف العدائية او الساخرة والشتائم لن نتساهل ولا يمكن القبول بها. ‎7. لاى عضو الحق في الابلاغ عن اي post او زميل اذا كسر اى من القواعد السابقة. ‎8. و الاجراءات سيجرى اتخاذها مع اى شخص يخالف النظام مهما كان. ‎9. وبما اننا نقدر الوقت ويود الجميع افضل تجربة مع الجروب. قبل نشر اى فكرة او موضوع جرب البحث فى تاريخ الجروب, ربما قد تم الرد او او تم عرض ما تريد. ‎10. يرجى الا تتردد فى ارسال مشاركتك او مشكلتك او اعترافاتكم الخاصه وستكون مجهول هوية صاحبها عن طريق اللينك دا https://www.facebook.com/groups/Confessionsofamarriedwoman/

           <div class="_8sz1 _8sz5 _8szd _8szj" id="u_0_62">
            <div class="_8t03 _8tm_">
             <a class="_8ulx" href="/groups/239433885078/">
              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Swedish American Genealogy Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 BASICS This is a way for Americans to search for Swedish roots or Swedes to find relatives in America. Queries, tips and interesting stories about ancestry. Commercials and spamming are not allowed. GENERAL ADVICE If you are looking for help, then a basic rule is to include as specific information as possible from the start of your thread. It is quite common that people start with very vague questions, but it turns out that they in fact have more information already. So please make it easier to help by making your queries as detailed as you can from the very beginning. Important information * Full name. Preferably also their swedish surname, to be able to find them in the passenger lists. For example, "Jack Lindbergh" could be the same person as Johan Petter Gustafsson, when you also have the information that his father's name probably was Gustaf. (patronymic) * Place of birth. Parish name and/or county. * Date of birth. In the 1900 Census you will find a year and month of birth. Other censuses provide an age, which gives an estimate of a year of birth. Death certificates often give full birthdates. * Date of emigration or Year of immigration. Can be found in the censuses of 1900 through 1930. * Destination in the US and where they lived in the US. (read more here: http://www.etgenealogy.se/krav.htm) INTEGRITY * You may only post information or data about deceased persons. Avoid posting information that can violate living persons. Do not post other people's e-mail addresses or contact information. * If the information is sensitive or extensive, a contact through PM or private e-mail is preferred. Please note that messages to persons, who are not on your friends list, will be sent to their "Other" inbox. REPLIES * Please check all previous comments before replying to a question, to see if it already has been answered. Sometimes you need to click on a link: "View more comments/Visa XX kommentarer till" to open all entries. Thank you! Admins: Mats Ahlgren Judy Olson Baouab Lori Ferguson Barbara Rasmussen Patrik Sassersson In Memoriam: Ingela Martenius, Nov 2018.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Sober Gay Single Men
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a closed Facebook group for people in recovery that self-identify as gay men. It is operated by Gay &amp; Sober. Gay &amp; Sober is a 501c3 nonprofit organization that serves members of the LGBTQ recovery community. ⭐️To find a meeting,visit: http://www.gayandsober.org/meetings This is a closed group for gay men in recovery so they can connect with each other when traveling, to keep in touch, dating, discuss sobriety, or just for fun. This is a Facebook group aimed at and supporting gay men in recovery from alcoholism and drug addiction. In the spirit of of love and service, please behave yourselves and practice principles before personalities. If you are adding a member, we suggest first asking them if they would like to be a member of this restored group. Then add them. We have some community guidelines: 1. 🚫No bullying. We will ban you. 2. 🚫When posting content, please relate it somehow to sobriety. For example: Just a shirtless selfie is NOT ok. But a shirtless selfie saying how glad you are to be fit and sober IS ok. 3. This group is for all forms of recovery. There are fellows from 12 step group, and non-12 step methods of recovery here. All are welcome. 🚫Criticizing or condemning people that are not staying sober the way you stay sober is not allowed. 4. 🚫Political posts are also discouraged. 5. 🚫No soliciting or crowdfunding (For example: GoFundMe) - unless it is for the nonprofit Gay &amp; Sober’s events and fundraising. ✋🏾We do encourage civil discussion however. And, if you're a former member of some method of staying sober - please don't use this forum to rant against any other method that someone on here might be using to live a sober life. It's not necessarily productive or polite. As this group continues to grow, so do the number of invitations to join from fake profiles, or people that should not be in this group. We try to screen the profiles, but from time to time some of this profiles make it in. ✔️MUST-DO TO JOIN: Your profile must have viewable information sufficient for us to know you're actually a human. Please understand that we are doing our best with this and we invite you to bring these matter's to an admin's attention as you see them. To get involved, please visit www.gayandsober.org/planning Thank you and enjoy our growing group! In Love &amp; Service, Gay &amp; Sober Social Networking www.gayandsober.org *Notification Warning: This is a very active group. Members are posting on here almost non-stop. If your inbox or Facebook notifications start exploding, be sure to click the "NOTIFICATIONS" buttons the top right of the page to turn them off. *A statement on Anonymity: This is Facebook. So obviously, we can see your full name and picture. Please be informed that ONLY fellow group members can see what other members post here. Outsiders can NOT see group posts or content. In short, anyone can find the group. Only members can see who's in it and what they post

               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Norwegian Genealogy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Founded: 27 April 2007. Purpose: to help one another learn how to research our Norwegian heritage and to find Norwegian ancestors as well as relatives Using Only PRINTED SOURCES. * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * Method: create a paper or digital documentation trail to specific individuals. Disclosures: our best answer to member research questions is to provide a link to the on-line documentation used as our sources for answers. Sometimes the question requires precise replies, facts and multiple sources in older forms of Norwegian. We try to teach the method we use to answer questions of others and in the process reveal the facts being sought often in Norwegian digital archives or other public records. Not allowed:: Use of genetic (DNA) matches as well as SNP or STR test results and GEDMATCH.com comparisons. When you join this Group, these are the rules. You and you alone may complete a request to join this closed Group, thus you are bound by our restrictions once accepted. 1. After clicking Join Group, check your OTHER mail on FB (i.e., sent by people who are not your FB friends yet) until you answer the Group Admin questions. You will be denied membership you take more than 72 hours to answer all questions. 2. If contacted by the Group admin via OTHER mail or otherwise, provide the information requested. Individuals who do not use their real name on FB or display no interest in Norwegian Genealogy on FB will always be asked for valid identification and/or reasons for joining this Group. Anyone who is blocking access to their public profile or FB messages will never be accepted to this group 3. Agree to never advertise a commercial product or service on this Group's pages Nor may you use information you gathered here for commercial gain. 4. Avoid political or religious proselytizing on this Group's pages. 5. Post detailed requests in English with full names, dates and most likely place or farm of people being sought. Several members may help you find answers. They post their replies in English in the thread below your question. Native Norwegians may also get help finding emigrants world-wide by posting similar details including known variations in names and dates of emigration if known and probable destinations; always use English. 6. Requests for translations of Norwegian should be short and directly related to one's family research. Photos or digitized documents should be directly related to the specific research subject of each thread. 7. Be polite, thankful and supportive of other members. Acknowledge support by posting replies and thanks in the same thread as your original question. Stick to the facts; avoid opinions and criticisms of others. -------------------------------- "Those who do not look upon themselves as links connecting the past with the future do not perform their duty to the world.“ Daniel Webster Group Type:Study/Research 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Western Armenian DNA Initiative (Republic of Armenia)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Note: this group's original purpose was related to collecting DNA from those of western Armenian extraction to contribute to the academic literature and post results that can then be utilized in larger project. However, as this group has evolved and my duties have changed, the scope of discussion has expanded and my purpose has shifted to expanding upon credible data related to our origins, whether human, or more specifically, as a population of humans called Armenians. What follows is the original description of the group and I find no need to edit it. Our intention is to create a fuller picture of the Armenian genome. Many studies within Armenia have been done on regional populations in the Republic, but to have a more complete spectrum of historic populations, we need input from Western Armenians. Most Diasporans can provide us with a better idea of the genomic footprint of Armenians within historic Armenia. We would like to collect saliva samples and cheek swaps to determine mitochondrial and Y-chromosome DNA. With the recent explosion of data available from Syrian Armenians, as well as repats, we can indeed have a desirable collection to obtain for analysis and genetic variation among Armenian groups. Please feel free to add those individuals that have a Western Armenian background. Please keep posts relevant to DNA and genetics. 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ginger Bears, Cubs and their admirers
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Ginger Bears/Cubs and their Admirers... (STRICTLY MEN ONLY GROUP) This article is about Bears with red hair, also sometimes called gingers. [1] Red hair (also referred to as titian or ginger hair) varies from a deep burgundy through burnt orange to bright copper. It is characterized by high levels of the reddish pigment pheomelanin and relatively low levels of the dark pigment eumelanin. [2] Bears with red hair are often referred to as redheads or gingers. Approximately 1% to 2% of the human population has red hair. It occurs more frequently (between 2% and 6% of the population) in northern and western Europeans, and their descendants, and at lower frequencies throughout other parts of the world. [3] Red hair appears in people with two copies of a recessive gene on chromosome 16 which causes a mutation in the MC1R protein. It is associated with fair skin color, lighter eye colors (gray, blue, green, and hazel), freckles, and sensitivity to ultraviolet light. [4] Cultural reactions have varied from ridicule to admiration; many common stereotypes exist regarding redheads and they are often portrayed as fiery-tempered. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Married Life...Real Talk
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is a train ride headed in EVERY direction with a stop for EVERYONE...if you feel like you are prepared for this ride - we welcome you aboard. The group is titled Married Life...Real Talk - this group is open to everyone - married or engaged ONLY please. We discuss ALL subjects and this group will answer and opinionate instantly...this is NOT strictly a support group...we offer opinionated advice only. So if you came here to have everyone agree with you then this might not be the group for you. On the other hand, we are also not here to judge one another...we realize that opinions are like assholes - everyone has one. Everyone will not like every post that's put up - for that reason, our mantra is "if it don't apply, scroll on by". Posts about what you thought this group was about or what you don't like about it will get you blocked. Our rules are simple and we expect everyone in the group to be respectful of them (not doing so will also get you blocked and deleted): 1. This is a group for those already married or engaged - it's not a hook up group. Find someplace else to do that. If we find out you are trolling member's inboxes you will be blocked and deleted immediately. 2. NO ADVERTISING!!! Don't come in here and post ads for your groups, books, outings, body wraps, clothing or food or any other services. 3. No gross nudity. Any post or meme containing any race degrading terms, illegal activities, or inappropriate material will be deleted. This is not your personal page so please don't treat it as such. 4. Be careful when you speak...and what you say to others. This is the age of the keyboard gangster and sometimes people can get beside themselves...when you feel like posts or threads are getting out of hand - PLEASE tag an admin. Or send us an IM. Don't continue on with messy conversations. And for the love of God, DO NOT troll people's pages and post that shit in this group. That get you swiftly blocked from this group. 5. Blocking of admins or moderators will get you blocked and deleted immediately 6. Reporting any posts to admin or Facebook is cause for immediate removal from the group. If you have an issue, take it up with an admin. 7. SCREENSHOTTING - you may post screenshots of scenarios from other groups. However - the name of the group MUST be cropped out along with any OP info...text only...but please be aware that someone may do the same to you...we don't have control over screenshotting...people do it all over the internet. Carol &amp; Hans Fritzgerald Latasha Frazier Hasan Ali Stephanie Johnson

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Strengthen Your Marriage
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Strengthen Your Marriage is a group sponsored by Married Fun - https://marriedfun.org - and intended for married people to come together and help each other. Members are here to support your marriage and marriage in general. Whether you are a newly-wed or have been married for decades; whether you are experiencing difficulties or are blissfully married, you will find support in your marriage by others who are here to help you succeed. If you are married and willing to learn and help others, you are in the right place. In joining this group you agree to abide by the following rules: GROUP RULES: • Introduce yourself - Tells us your age, length of marriage and location along with anything else you'd like us to know. • Support each other - The group exists for pro marriage people to support one another. • Keep it respectful - No name calling, foul language, profanity, bullying or judgy behavior. Those who are overly negative, bashing others and similar will be removed. This isn't a forum for fringe or divisive political, religious or racial talk. Express your opinions but be prepared to agree to disagree. • Keep it clean - No nude or sexually explicit content. • This is not your free advertising forum. Minimal promotion of related resources may be offered, but only if they embody the rules and intent of this group. If you're looking to get the word out about your product or service, contact an admin. • Off-topic content should be kept to a minimum. • Please be active. Help us grow by adding your married friends who you think might be interested in being a part of us. • Honor each others' marriages - Actions, solicitations and conduct detrimental to someone else's marriage will not be tolerated. TIPS FOR SUCCESS: • Make sure you allow notifications from the group. • Be active in the group - ask questions and answer other peoples' questions. • Invite your married friends to join or share our group. • Don't forget to LIKE our official facebook page and check out our service, Married Fun. https://marriedfun.org/ https://www.facebook.com/marriedfun.org/ YOU BELONG HERE IF: • You are married • You will support others in strengthening their marriages • You fill follow the group rules NOTE: This is an Open Group, which means discussions are visible to both group members and other users. This group is for Married Couples Only, please don't invite minors, singles, swingers, etc. - there are plenty of places for them to congregate. We want to maintain a group of like-minded people who are better equipped to support one another. We reserve the right to remove any posted content that we feel is inappropriate or contrary to our image at any time. Violators of the group rules will be removed. We are not responsible for the content that members post to this group. Posted content should not be regarded as professional or medical advice. We will amend the group rules at any time we feel is appropriate.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 International Society of Genetic Genealogy (ISOGG)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "The mission of the International Society of Genetic Genealogy is to advocate for and educate about the use of genetics as a tool for genealogical research, and promote a supportive network for genetic genealogists." Welcome new members! Please read through the group rules below. Group Rules: Be kind and considerate; treat others the way you'd want to be treated (including the DNA companies). Stay on the group's topic; no religious posts, and no partisan political bashing. The only political posts allowed are when it relates to DNA legislation, but keep partisan bashing out of it. Commercial genetic genealogy postings ARE allowed, but grandstanding is not. Grandstanding is when you complain about a company or other commercial entity (i.e.: a consultant, etc.) and you have not contacted them with your issues and grievances first so they can address it. If you do on-list grandstanding, you may be asked to provide correspondence with company or person you are complaining about. Grandstanding posts will be deleted by the admins. As the name of the group states, ISOGG's focus is on using DNA for GENEALOGY. Anthropology-related posts will be allowed as long as any comments do not devolve into contentiousness. Debating theories or the semantics of population labels are off-topic in this group and will be deleted. Law Enforcement (LE) or Investigative Genealogy posts are allowed but commenting needs to be turned off. Join CeCe Moore's Investigative Genealogy Facebook group for this topic. Do not block any of the admins. We need to be able to respond to posts and "see" you (and you us) in order to properly administer this group and efficiently help the other posters. Those who block ISOGG Group Admins will be removed from the group. Please use the "Report to Admin" link and NOT the "Report to Facebook" link to report a post. Otherwise, your Admins have no idea what's being reported; we are just sent a notice that something has been reported. If it's porn or sunglasses ads, then that's quite understandable, but if it's even remotely related to the list topic, we would prefer to be the judges of it as opposed to some Facebook computer bot who does the judging. The group itself is not the appropriate place to question, debate, or comment on the group rules or the way that the Admins run the group. If you have questions or feedback on group rules and how they are applied, send a private message to the admins. Violations of these rules may result in being removed and blocked. Further recommended reading on appropriate netiquette for this group, read: http://www.rootsandrecombinantdna.com/2017/08/genetic-genealogy-forums-online.html

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Black &amp; White Men Together, Nat. Assn. of: A Gay Multiracial Org for All
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 “NABWMT Envisions Creating Equitable Educational and Social Spaces that Move Past Racial and Cultural Barriers.” (approved, Feb., 2016 by the Board of Directors) This NABWMT Face Book page is NOT DESIGNED as a pick-up, hook up/sex site, or for selling merchandise (unless it's OUR own). If you attempt to solicit sex or peddle merchandise, we will delete your post(s). If you use a silly pseudonym (false name), or if you post in a different language without English translation, or if you have not personally demonstrated interest in LGBT, racial/cultural issues, or other issues consistent with our Statement of Purpose (below), know that: THIS IS THE BEST WAY TO INSURE THAT YOUR POST WILL BE DELETED AND YOU REMOVED FROM THE GROUP. Please: No "How's it going," or sexually explicit or suggestive photos. If you find yourself repeatedly posting things that are NOT broadcast to the group, contact administrators (see below) and we will explain why your posts are being deleted, and more importantly, how you can get your posts properly displayed! Thanks for your understanding! The National Association of Black and White Men Together: A Gay Multiracial Organization for All People (NABWMT) is a tax exempt, gay, multiracial, multicultural organization committed to fostering supportive environments wherein racial and cultural barriers can be overcome and the goal of human equality realized. To these ends we engage in educational, political, cultural and social activities as a means of dealing with the racism, sexism, homophobia, HIV/AIDS discrimination and other inequities in our communities and in our lives. Local chapters exist throughout the country with the name "Black and White Men Together (BWMT)," "Men of All Colors Together (MACT)," "Men of All Cultures and Colors Together (MACCT)," "People of All Colors Together (PACT)," "Friends of All Colors Together (FACT)," or variations thereof. Seven cities have local chapters with scheduled activities: Atlanta, Milwaukee, Seattle, Long Beach/Los Angeles/Southern California, Philadelphia, Phoenix, South Florida/Ft. Lauderdale. Several previous chapters remain socially active together but have evolved into less formally structured organizations (Denver, Detroit, Chicago, New York, San Diego). Interested in finding out more? Joining a local chapter? Forming a chapter? Contact us! We value your membership and your active participation locally, globally, and especially during our National Convention!! Current administrators/moderators are mostly current or past members of the NABWMT Board of Directors, and include: Sat: Gavin Morrow-Hall (SF); Sun: Mike Spears (Atlanta); Mon: Darryl Fore (Cleveland); Tue: Mark Behar (Milwaukee); Wed: Patrick Carron (Ft. Lauderdale/SoFL); Thur: Rick Gile-Creque; Fri: Kirk Gile-Creque &amp; Ken Scott Baron (Long Beach/SoCA). We'd love to hear from you, and how we together can work together to achieve our goals. NABWMT, P.O.B. 3793, Hollywood, CA 90078-3793.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 MISSION :Learning to accept all the physical and emotional changes that come with being gay and over 60 . . THIS IS A SAFE HAVEN FOR EVERYONE Over 60 Go ahead and introduce yourself! Keep it short and sweet. Give us a sense of who you are, where you live, what makes you tick, or what you’re searching for in life or in this group. RULES : This page is not a hook-up site! The group doesn't allow postings of the following: 1) We can’t stress this enough — this is a place for open-hearted discussion and encouragement. Disagreement is natural and welcome; however, NO DEROGATORY/DEMEANING STATEMENTS, COMMENTS, OR REBUTTALS. BULLYING IS NOT ALLOWED. 2) Generalized statements of any city locations. If asking about a generalized city or region, please expand on why. 3) No posting phone numbers. We do not want to give out numbers, besides the fact that it's dangerous for you. If you have yours posted in your account, keep it there and let members know privately for the safety of the staff, members, and Facebook itself. 4) Limiting public friendship requests, we are not looking to date, let's all try to be friends. IF you wish to contact a person please inbox them privately. If you're looking for a date, check out GAY LIFE AFTER 40 FOR DATING separately. 5) ALL illegal substance requests, posts or questions will be removed without question or notice. 6) Only approved advertising will be allowed. PLEASE MAKE SURE ALL ADS HAVE AGE REQUIREMENTS ON THEM. LIKE BARS! 7) Pictures - Due to increased scrutiny by Facebook prompted by carelessness of past members, we ask that you please be fully clothed from the waist down.. This is not the place for nude or seductive pictures of you or any objects.. A photo or post can be deleted without notice. Membership could be removed. 8) Political Talk-We want our members to get away from politics so we can talk about other topics. Feel free to join other groups that discuss politics on a daily basis--this is not the group. LEGAL NOTE : Any advice or suggestions given to or from any members from or given to any administrators of this group is purely at the discretion of said member or administrator. The group, staff, and members are not at any liability to give any consultation or receive any and are here by exempt from any legal actions.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Love quotes for you
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Love is about caring and healing. When we love someone truly, we want to see them grow and flourish. But if you start to have negative feelings towards the same person because they cannot become a part of your life, the love was not true in the first place. Love is emotion and we can have these emotions for anyone. Sometimes we have emotions for those who can never be ours. When people realise this, at times these emotions become even more intense because mind wants what you can’t have. But love should never turn into rage or feeling of destruction. Love will always want you to be safe and protected. Love is about peace and joy whether you have them or not. Only if your love heals, it’s true love. ❤️ if you want to get inspirational, motivational and encouraging messages on telegram too then feel free to join telegram group 👇 https://t.me/joinchat/UzMeJxxPEaLD8-kMLxustQ 🥀🌸 🥀🌸 🥀🌸 ❤️ Don't forget to Like My Page to Read positive and Inspirational posts https://www.facebook.com/zeeshansiddiquezee Follow me on Twitter 👇 https://twitter.com/Heeero711 Follow me on Instagram👇 https://www.instagram.com/zeeshansiddiquezee/ Stay happy and cool! love you all 💗 -Zee

By joining this group, you understand that spam posts are not permitted. Links that are posted to outside pages, websites or anything else, without approval from an admin or the group owner, are prohibited and will not be approved for posting. Failure to comply with the above will result in immediate removal from BBCP. No exceptions! Formerly known as Blue Bears, Cubs and Pandas, BBCP Bears Worldwide has over 12,000 followers on Facebook. We exist on other social media platforms such as Twitter, Instagram, and Tumblr. We are a group dedicated to the diversity within the various bear communities across the globe.                <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Scottish Genealogy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The idea behind the group is for general help with research in to Scottish genealogy as and when each of us (the members of this group) can. This help can be: 1 Finding potential family connections This could be from one of the many websites, Primarily Scotlands People as your first point of call.Facebook groups, etc. or at the National Records of Scotland in Edinburgh.It is always worth cross referencing with other websites such as Ancestry and Family Search .but do remember these sites should only be used as a guide..."PAPER TRAIL" is the key. Also, while doing this kind of research, you naturally find other details (through census, birth, etc records) that are not related to yourself; you never know when someone might be looking for something you already have or maybe someone has something you are looking for. Keeping a log of all this extra info wouldn't really take much time (even if it just a note of names and general locations such as parish or town). Additionally people might have books that give some family details or know of books/authors that cover certain areas. 2 Helping to decipher family records already discovered (which, in all honesty, at first glance are not always easy to read). 3 Visiting (and getting names) from grave yards and war memorials. It is initially this documented info that I am looking to be shared within the groups. While there are many genealogy websites available for further research, unfortunately a lot of those allow people to create links without providing any evidence for them (hence the reason a lot of people might find they are related to someone famous, such as royalty, and while many of them are happy to take that as gospel I would rather avoid that sort of thing - or at least, as nicely as possible, point out that what they have found may not be genuine). Please also note that this group is for posts and queries in connection with family research; if anyone is looking to find out about Scotland in general there are many other Scottish FB pages you can join....Happy Hunting
                </div>
