               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Prussian Genealogy / German &amp; Polish Roots, DNA, Culture &amp; History
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Prussian Genealogy! Willkommen in der Gruppe, “Ahnenforschung in Preußen!” To join this group, you will be asked 3 questions. If you do not answer them satisfactorily, you will be denied membership. ***MISSION*** We are a global &amp; supportive community whose principal focus is dedicated to Prussian Genealogy. We also promote German and Polish genealogy, DNA, history, geography, culture &amp; other aspects as they relate to historical Prussia. We are happy to assist members whose Germanic, Polish or other roots do not technically fall within historical Prussia. We may either perform research help or point members in the right direction. You will find volunteers who are very willing and eager to help out members with research queries. Our community also cultivates a culture of self-education during the family research process. While many of our members are English speakers, we welcome persons from other linguistic backgrounds as well! ***PRUSSIA*** Historical Prussia chiefly applies to an immense area consisting of parts of modern Germany &amp; Poland. However, Prussian control extended also into portions of Lithuania, Russia &amp; Denmark as well. Due to historical Prussia’s constantly-changing borders, Prussian Genealogy can be confusing at times. Do not hesitate to ask any geographical or historical questions that you may have ****RULES*** Our Admin team offers our unwavering commitment to strive to ensure that all members feel comfortable and welcome here!!! We reserve the right to delete any comments &amp; posts that do not conform to our community's rules or mission. As a general rule, a member will be warned once for a non-confrontational group violation. If a member violates the same rule a second time, he or she will be removed from our community. On the other hand, if a member is intentionally divisive, he or she will be automatically removed from our community without a warning. ***Posts, comments &amp; stickers that involve any form of negativity, name-calling, arguing, gossiping, toxic or snarky behavior or political, sexual, racist, spammy content or research concerning living persons or cross-posting are completely unacceptable and no warning given. Thanks for your cooperation! ***PARTICIPATION*** We are glad to assist members with their Prussian family research. When posting a research query, please share as many details, docs and URL links, as necessary, in your original post. Members may pursue connections, share their research brick walls, breakthroughs, stories, pictures, videos, &amp; other content (e.g., humor that is in good taste)---but, they all must be related in some way to Prussian (or German or Polish) Genealogy, DNA, history, geography &amp; culture. Our community participates in the DNA Matchmaker &amp; the Gedmatch Ancestor Project. Many of our resources &amp; ways to connect with other members can be found in Announcements section (pinned post area) at the top of our site. Happy Prussian Genealogy!
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Association of Transgender Professionals
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 &gt;&gt;&gt; ALL Members Should Read This BEFORE Posting &lt;&lt;&lt; Without financial equality, there can be no equality. This is an association of people who have, had or will have non-conforming gender expressions/identities and seek to advance their professional careers. The goal of this group is to facilitate the networking and mentoring which develop our careers and promote the next generation of leaders. There are 3 criteria for membership: 1) You get paid for what you do or you want to get paid. 2) You who have, had or will have non-conforming gender expression and/or identity. 3) You want to associate with people who meet criteria #1 and criteria #2. Live by the Golden Rule and treat others as you would want to be treated. Show Respect for the Individual at all times, even in the face of adversity and disrespect. Please keep the focus on the workplace and our careers. Refrain from posting about politics, news articles, links, and stories that don't directly apply to the workplace experience. This means that all posts must be directly workplace-related and if the direct connection is unclear, it is the responsibility of the poster to explain the direct connection. Posts that are not directly connected to the workplace or lack an explanation if the connection is unclear may be removed without prior warning. By directly connection, we mean that the post is about the workplace in some manner. Example: A law is passed that prohibits local anti-workplace discrimination laws. An indirect connection is about something that affects something else that eventually impacts the workplace. Example: A law is passed that allows taxi drivers to refuse service to people on religious grounds which could ultimately delay an unknown number of gender diverse people from getting to work. However, a post about a gender diverse employee who loses their job because their job is dependent on riding in taxis would be a direct connection. Also, if a post is deleted because the direct workplace connection is not clear, the original poster is welcome to repost and make the connection clear in their comments. Occasional general event postings are welcome provided they clearly support our community. Occasional advertising for services, products, events offered, created or managed by members are also welcome. The value we get out of this group starts with the quality of what we put into the group This group is OPEN and everyone can see who is a member and what is being posted, even if they are not a member of the group. This allows the wisdom and experience shared here to be available to everyone --- especially those whose privacy needs may prevent them from disclosing their gender identity or history to employers, family and/or friends. Group Administrators ------------------------------- Denise Norris Jenna Fischetti Kelly Ellis Avery Sudol

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Whoops, sorry, it's gay now! Post the accidental-but-undeniable LGBTQ+ representation that you find around the web or offline. This group is free to join and leave! Add anyone you think would find this fun! Straight cis people can join and contribute, but be respectful &amp; extra careful about basing the 'evidence' on stereotypes. Please try not to start any discourse; this is a lighthearted joke group and there are many other groups around for discussion of political ideologies and intracommunity issues. If you believe something is not right, please tag a mod. We try to assume good intentions and give the benefit of the doubt, but will absolutely not accept any -isms/-phobias or jackassery. You will be warned and then, if you do not heed the warning and keep being A Jackass, banned. Please read and answer all questions before requesting to join. If you don’t understand a question, please message a mod or admin. Certain topics for posts require content warnings. If your post is missing one of these CWs it WILL NOT be approved. You may include CWs that are not on this list. If another member requests that you add a content warning, do so. Here are the required CWs: - Homophobia, transphobia*, bipobia, panphobia, aphobia, exorsexism, interphobia, any queerphobia.** - Sex or genital mention, even implied. This includes top/bottom jokes. - Anything else NSFW - Any slurs** - Self harm or suicide - Drugs or alcohol, including weed - Abuse (specify if sexual abuse) - Surgery or medical transition - Menstruation - Pregnancy - Eating disorders, fatphobia, etc. - Violence, gore, or death - Religious content - Racism, sexism, ableism, or any other bigotry (but don't be surprised if a post including any of this doesn't get approved) * For transphobia, please be specific if possible. Examples include but are not limited to: transmisogyny, bioessentialism, and misgendering. ** Note, people do not have to censor their own identities. The CW is necessary when original post or content was -phobic and was posted here in a reclaiming way. Happy repspotting!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Genealogical Translations
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 JOIN REQUESTS: Approval based on reply to 1 question &amp; selecting “I agree” after reading the group rules. This group helps members with translation of their genealogical documents. Volunteers offer free translation of genealogical documents including vital records, postcards, obituaries, and more, in languages including – Dutch, French, German, Hebrew, Hungarian, Italian, Latin, Polish, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish, and many others! Translations are offered by members located worldwide, who volunteer their knowledge and time. We welcome all members wishing to volunteer their assistance. This group does NOT: ▶ Offer assistance with transcription of genealogical documents in ENGLISH. Please join the “Deciphering Genealogy Script” Facebook group for help. https://www.facebook.com/groups/672462506205064/ ▶ Provide general genealogical research services. Genealogical research related questions may be directed to one of the groups/pages found in the “Genealogy on Facebook” List. https://socialmediagenealogy.com/genealogy-on-facebook-list/ ▶ Translate documents unrelated to genealogy. ▶ Translate documents for legal purposes. ▶ Translate documents to be used for commercial enterprises. Note: Members are encouraged to help other members, although we cannot vouch for anyone’s expertise. Advertising or otherwise promoting paid services is not allowed in this group. Professional genealogists may not ask for assistance on paid work however you may request translation of genealogical documents related to your own personal ancestry. 
                </div>
               </div>

We four main rules about posting (subject to change or be altered at will by the Admin team): 1. No marketing of ANY kind on the main timeline. This includes business, blogs, other pages, sermons, live videos, conferences, trips, or personal videos/posts promoting your business/brand. With that being said, please keep financial things outside of the group, to include aboved metioned items as wellas subjects such as taxes and serious financial decisions concerning your family. 2. Intimacy questions are at admin discretion and may be deleted if the content is explicit or if it becomes that way at any point on the thread. 4. Respect one another at ALL TIMES! We have tons of people from different walks of life and backgrounds, so naturally we don’t all do marriage the same way. Agree to disagree and move on! Also when posting please do not include screenshots or pictures of other spouse’s activity, etc. Post may be immediately deleted. There are NO exceptions to these rules, you may be blocked/delted with no explanation as it is your responsibility to be informed of the groups rules. Please keep memes to a minimal, and always remember this is NOT your personal page but a group to discuss marriage things, good and bad, so me mindful of the content you post in relation to marriage. Personal message from B Lee (group creator): I look forward to growing in love with each and every one of you all. Also , if you already have a group, or starting a group. PLEASE DO NOT POST IT HERE.... You will be deleted and blocked!
